Including many bloody reprisals, The total death toll was in the range of 10,000 to 30,000.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/William_Pitt_the_Younger" title="William Pitt the Younger">William Pitt the Younger</a>, the British prime minister, firmly believed that the only solution to the problem was a union of Great Britain and Ireland.  The union was established by the <a href="/wiki/Act_of_Union_1800" class="mw-redirect" title="Act of Union 1800">Act of Union 1800</a>; compensation and <a href="/wiki/Patronage" title="Patronage">patronage</a> ensured the support of the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Ireland" title="Parliament of Ireland">Irish Parliament</a>. Great Britain and Ireland were formally united on 1 January 1801.  The Irish Parliament was closed down.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Monarchs">Monarchs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kingdom_of_Great_Britain&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Monarchs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_(1714-1801).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_%281714-1801%29.svg/100px-Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_%281714-1801%29.svg.png" width="100" height="117" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_%281714-1801%29.svg/150px-Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_%281714-1801%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_%281714-1801%29.svg/200px-Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_%281714-1801%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="410" data-file-height="478" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Arms_of_Great_Britain_(1714-1801).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms" title="Coat of arms">coat of arms</a> of the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Hanover" title="House of Hanover">House of Hanover</a></div></div></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="House_of_Stuart">House of Stuart</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kingdom_of_Great_Britain&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: House of Stuart">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Anne,_Queen_of_Great_Britain" title="Anne, Queen of Great Britain">Anne</a> (1707\xe2\x80\x931714) (previously <a href="/wiki/Queen_regnant" title="Queen regnant">Queen of England</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Scottish_monarchs" title="List of Scottish monarchs">Queen of Scots</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Queen_of_Ireland" class="mw-redirect" title="Queen of Ireland">Queen of Ireland</a> since 1702)</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="House_of_Hanover">House of Hanover</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kingdom_of_Great_Britain&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: House of Hanover">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/George_I_of_Great_Britain" title="George I of Great Britain">George I</a> (1714\xe2\x80\x931727)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/George_II_of_Great_Britain" title="George II of Great Britain">George II</a> (1727\xe2\x80\x931760)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/George_III_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="George III of the United Kingdom">George III</a> (1760\xe2\x80\x931801) (continued as King of the United Kingdom until his death in 1820)</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Parliament_of_Great_Britain">Parliament of Great Britain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kingdom_of_Great_Britain&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Parliament of Great Britain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Great_Britain" title="Parliament of Great Britain">Parliament of Great Britain</a> and <a href="/wiki/Elections_in_Great_Britain" title="Elections in Great Britain">Elections in Great Britain</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:William_Pitt_addressing_the_House_of_Commons_on_the_outbreak_of_war_with_Austria_(by_Karl_Anton_Hickel).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/97/William_Pitt_addressing_the_House_of_Commons_on_the_outbreak_of_war_with_Austria_%28by_Karl_Anton_Hickel%29.jpg/250px-William_Pitt_addressing_the_House_of_Commons_on_the_outbreak_of_war_with_Austria_%28by_Karl_Anton_Hickel%29.jpg" width="250" height="177" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/97/William_Pitt_addressing_the_House_of_Commons_on_the_outbreak_of_war_with_Austria_%28by_Karl_Anton_Hickel%29.jpg/375px-William_Pitt_addressing_the_House_of_Commons_on_the_outbreak_of_war_with_Austria_%28by_Karl_Anton_Hickel%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/9/97/William_Pitt_addressing_the_House_of_Commons_on_the_outbreak_of_war_with_Austria_%28by_Karl_Anton_Hickel%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="410" data-file-height="291" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:William_Pitt_addressing_the_House_of_Commons_on_the_outbreak_of_war_with_Austria_(by_Karl_Anton_Hickel).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/William_Pitt_the_Younger" title="William Pitt the Younger">Pitt</a> addressing the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_Great_Britain" title="House of Commons of Great Britain">Commons</a> in 1793</div></div></div>\n<p>The Parliament of Great Britain consisted of the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Lords" title="House of Lords">House of Lords</a> (an unelected upper house of the <a href="/wiki/Lords_Spiritual" title="Lords Spiritual">Lords Spiritual</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lords_Temporal" title="Lords Temporal">Temporal</a>) and the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_Great_Britain" title="House of Commons of Great Britain">House of Commons</a>, the lower chamber, which was elected periodically. In <a href="/wiki/England_and_Wales" title="England and Wales">England and Wales</a> parliamentary constituencies remained unchanged throughout the existence of the Parliament.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>During the 18th century, the <a href="/wiki/British_Constitution" class="mw-redirect" title="British Constitution">British Constitution</a> developed significantly.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Peerage_of_Great_Britain">Peerage of Great Britain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kingdom_of_Great_Britain&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Peerage of Great Britain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Peerage_of_Great_Britain" title="Peerage of Great Britain">Peerage of Great Britain</a></div>\n<p>As a result of the Union of 1707, no new <a href="/wiki/Peerage" title="Peerage">peerages</a> were created in the <a href="/wiki/Peerage_of_England" title="Peerage of England">Peerage of England</a> or the <a href="/wiki/Peerage_of_Scotland" title="Peerage of Scotland">Peerage of Scotland</a>. English peerages continued to carry the right to a seat in the House of Lords, while the Scottish peers elected <a href="/wiki/Representative_peers" class="mw-redirect" title="Representative peers">representative peers</a> from among their own number to sit in the Lords. Peerages continued to be created by <a href="/wiki/The_Crown" title="The Crown">the Crown</a>, either in the new <a href="/wiki/Peerage_of_Great_Britain" title="Peerage of Great Britain">Peerage of Great Britain</a>, which was that of the new kingdom and meant a seat in its House of Lords, or in the <a href="/wiki/Peerage_of_Ireland" title="Peerage of Ireland">Peerage of Ireland</a>, giving the holder a seat in the <a href="/wiki/Irish_House_of_Lords" title="Irish House of Lords">Irish House of Lords</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Historiography">Historiography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kingdom_of_Great_Britain&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Historiography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Historiography_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Historiography of the United Kingdom">historiography of the United Kingdom</a> and <a href="/wiki/Historiography_of_the_British_Empire" title="Historiography of the British Empire">historiography of the British Empire</a></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kingdom_of_Great_Britain&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Great_Britain_in_the_Seven_Years%27_War" title="Great Britain in the Seven Years&#39;
